(<tam>குறள்</tam>.) <p2><tam>சோகாப்பு</tam>, <i>v. noun.</i> Languishing, fainting, sorrow, grief.</p2></p> </blockquote>
		</div>

Astrological or astronomical writings.</p2> <p2><tam>சோதிடசாத்திரர்</tam>–<tam>சோதிடநூலோர்</tam> –<tam>சோதிடர்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Astrologers and astronomers.</p2> <p2><tam>சோதிடம்பார்க்க</tam>, <i>inf.</i> To consult astrology to find out a lucky day or hour, or to ascertain the fortune of a child.</p2> <p2><tam>சோதிடவாதம்</tam>, <i>s. [vul.]</i> A system of religion which regards the heavenly bodies as supreme, and as having the control over and management of all things, and which considers astronomy and astrology as the highest knowledge. <tam>சோதிடமார்க்கம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>சோதிடவாதி</tam>, <i>s.</i> A professor of the planetary religion.</p2></p> </blockquote>

See <tam>முச்சுடர்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>சோமசேகரன்</tam>–<tam>சோமநாதன்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Siva, as worshipped at Somnauth, <tam>சிவன்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>சோமமணல்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Sand containing silver, <tam>வெள்ளிமணல்</tam>. <i>(R.)</i></p2> <p2><tam>சோமமண்டலம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The region, orbit or disc of the man.</p2> <p2><tam>சோமலிங்கம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The <tam>இலிங்கம்</tam> of Siva, as worshipped by Soma or the moon at <tam>சோமாரணியம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>சோமலிங்கர்</tam>, <i>s. (Hon.)</i> Siva as worshipped at <tam>சோமாரணியம்</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>சோமவாரம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Monday. <i>(Colloq.)</i></p2> <p2><tam>சோமனுப்பு</tam>, <i>s.</i> Rock-salt, as <tam>இந்துப்பு</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>சோமன்சாம்பு</tam>–<tam>சோமன்மடி</tam>, <i>s. [loc.]</i> A piece containing several cloths or handkerchiefs for men. See <tam>சாம்பு</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>சோமன்சோடு</tam>, <i>s.</i> A cloth and shawl, the two forming a common dress; one twelve, the other six cubits. <i>(c.)</i></p2> <p2><tam>சோமாரணியம்</tam>, <i>s.</i> The forest where the moon made <i>puja</i> to the Siva Linga, <tam>ஓர் சிவஸ்தலம்</tam>; [<i>ex</i> <tam>ஆரணியம்</tam>.]</p2> <p2><tam>சோமேசுரன்</tam>, <i>s.</i> Siva as worshipped by the moon, <tam>சிவன்</tam>; [<i>ex</i> <tam>ஈசுரன்</tam>.]</p2> <p2><tam>பட்டுக்கரைச்சோமன்</tam>, <i>s.</i> A <tam>சோமன்</tam> cloth with a silk border. <i>(c.)</i></p2> <p2><tam>பிள்ளைச்சோமன்</tam>, <i>s.</i> A small cloth for a boy.</p2></p> </blockquote>

[prov.]</i> To swell or enlarge, as rice in boiling.</p2> <p2><tam>சோறுவடிக்க</tam>, <i>inf.</i> To strain off rice.</p2> <p2><tam>சோறூட்டல்</tam>, <i>v. noun.</i> The ceremony of first feeding with rice, performed on an auspicious day. [prov.]</i> See <tam>குடலை</tam>.</p2> <p2><tam>சோற்றுக்குவீங்கி</tam>, <i>appel. n.</i> A man greedy of food, who will eat any where.</p2> <p2><tam>சோற்றுக்கூடை</tam>, <i>s.</i> A large basket in which rice is served up to a company.</p2> <p2><tam>சோற்றுக்கை</tam>, <i>s.</i> The right hand as used in eating rice, &c.–oppos. to <tam>பீச்சைக்கை</tam>. <i>(c.)</i></p2> <p2><tam>சோற்றுக்கொடை</tam>, <i>s.</i> Giving boiled rice as alms to religious mendicants, being the first kind of bounty.</p2> <p2><tam>சோற்றுச்சட்டி</tam>, <i>s.</i> An earthen pan for cooling boiled rice.</p2> <p2><tam>சோற்றுத்துருத்தி</tam>, <i>s.</i> The body; <i>(lit.)</i> a leather bag of rice. <i>(p.)</i></p2> <p2><tam>சோற்றுநித்திரை</tam>–<tam>சோற்றுறக்கம்</tam>, <i>s. <script src="/dictionaries/bootstrap/bootstrap.min.js"></script>

<script>

    $(document).ready(function(){
        $(document).keypress(function(event) {
                var keycode = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
                if (keycode == "116") {
                        var selection = window.getSelection().toString();
			var q_param = $.trim(selection);
			q_param = q_param.replace(/[;]/g, '%3B');
			var q_param = q_param.replace(/\/?#/g,'')
			//console.log(selection)
			//console.log(q_param)
			var q_url = 'tamil/get_transliteration.py?q=' + q_param;
			$.ajax({
				url:q_url,
				dataType: "text"
			}).done(function(data){
				//console.log(data)
				var title_text = selection.replace(/\u00a0\u00a0/g,'\u00a0') 
				title_text = title_text.replace(/\u00a0/g,'<br/>')
				var title = '<span id="transliteration_modal_override">Transliteration for: ' + title_text + '</span>';
				var display_data = '<span id="transliteration_modal_override">' + data + '</span>';
				$('#tranliterationModal').find('.modal-title').html(title);
				$('#tranliterationModal').find('.modal-body').html(display_data);
				$('#tranliterationModal').modal('show');
			}).fail(function(xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
				console.log(xhr)
				console.log(ajaxOptions)
				console.log(thrownError)
				if (thrownError === 'Request-URI Too Long') {
					var message = "Please select a smaller passage to transliterate";
				}
				else if (thrownError === 'Internal Server Error') {
					var message = "The transliteration code encountered a problem. Please try again.";
				}
				var title = "Error: " + thrownError;
				//var message = "Please select a smaller passage to transliterate";
				$('#tranliterationModal').find('.modal-title').text(title);
				$('#tranliterationModal').find('.modal-body').text(message);
				$('#tranliterationModal').modal('show');
			});
                };
        });
    });

</script>

</body>
</html>
